      $(document).ready(function () {

      function createAbortPopup(eventId, armyType) {
          let target = armyType === 'spy' ?
              '?action=Espionage&function=abortSpyTraining&cityId=6581&eid=' + eventId +
              '&actionRequest=17ff1227542cc683a423dc61824682ab&position=1' :
              '?action=CityScreen&function=abortMilitaryConstruction&cityId=6581&actionRequest=17ff1227542cc683a423dc61824682ab&position=1&eid=' + eventId + '&type=' + armyType;
  
          ikariam.createPopup("abortPopup", '',
              ['Tens certeza que queres cancelar a construção deste edifício? Perderás todos os recursos que investiste!',
                  target,
                  'Sim', 'Abortar'], 1);
      }
  
      function recruitmentSpeedUpCall() {
          var selectedValue = $('.js_reduceItemSelect').val();
          var inventory = [];
          if (parseInt(selectedValue) === 0 || !inventory[selectedValue]) {
              return;
          }
          var url = inventory[selectedValue]['activationUrl'];
          ajaxHandlerCall(url);
      }
  </script>

  <div id="mainview">
      <script type="text/javascript">
  
          /* TODO:
           maybe live-update happiness-smiley-faces.
           track freeGoods
           expand/contract each slider to min(museum level, currentValue+freeGoods).
           */
  
          var satisfactionPerTreaty = 50;
  
          var satisfactionLevels = new Array(
              -1000,
              -50,
              0,
              50,
              300        );
  
          var satisfactionClasses = new Array(
              'satisfaction outraged',
              'satisfaction sad',
              'satisfaction neutral',
              'satisfaction happy',
              'satisfaction ecstatic'
          );
  
          var satisfactionTexts = new Array(
              'furioso',
              'miserável',
              'indiferente',
              'contente',
              'eufórico'
          );
  
          var basicSatisfaction = new Array();
  
  
          function getHappyness(satisfaction) {
  
              if (satisfaction > satisfactionLevels[4]) {
                  return 4;
              }
              else if (satisfaction > satisfactionLevels[3] && satisfaction <= satisfactionLevels[4]) {
                  return 3;
              }
              else if (satisfaction >= satisfactionLevels[2] && satisfaction <= satisfactionLevels[3]) {
                  return 2;
              }
              else if (satisfaction > satisfactionLevels[1] && satisfaction < satisfactionLevels[2]) {
                  return 1;
              }
              else {
                  return 0;
              }
          }
  
  
          function cDisplay() {
              var that = this;
              var registeredSliders = new Array();
              var iniValues = new Array();
              var iniMaxValues = new Array();
              var freeGoods =0;
              var totalAmount = freeGoods;
              var displayTotal = $("#cgAmount");

          /* TODO:
           maybe live-update happiness-smiley-faces.

          var satisfactionPerTreaty = 50;
  
          var satisfactionLevels = new Array(
              -1000,
              -50,
              0,
              50,
              300        );
  
          var satisfactionClasses = new Array(
              'satisfaction outraged',
              'satisfaction sad',
              'satisfaction neutral',
              'satisfaction happy',
              'satisfaction ecstatic'
          );
  
          var satisfactionTexts = new Array(
              'furioso',
              'miserável',
              'indiferente',
              'contente',
              'eufórico'
          );
  
          var basicSatisfaction = new Array();
  
  
          function getHappyness(satisfaction) {
  
              if (satisfaction > satisfactionLevels[4]) {
                  return 4;
              }
              else if (satisfaction > satisfactionLevels[3] && satisfaction <= satisfactionLevels[4]) {
                  return 3;
              }
              else if (satisfaction >= satisfactionLevels[2] && satisfaction <= satisfactionLevels[3]) {
                  return 2;
              }
              else if (satisfaction > satisfactionLevels[1] && satisfaction < satisfactionLevels[2]) {
                  return 1;
              }
              else {
                  return 0;
              }
          }

      $(document).ready(function () {
          getCountdown({
              enddate: '1774938663',

      function createAbortPopup(eventId, armyType) {
          let target = armyType === 'spy' ?
              '?action=Espionage&function=abortSpyTraining&cityId=6581&eid=' + eventId +
              '&actionRequest=ecc5dee7cab5482b3d4babb6f36b4d28&position=11' :
              '?action=CityScreen&function=abortMilitaryConstruction&cityId=6581&actionRequest=ecc5dee7cab5482b3d4babb6f36b4d28&position=11&eid=' + eventId + '&type=' + armyType;
  
          ikariam.createPopup("abortPopup", '',
              ['Tens certeza que queres cancelar a construção deste edifício? Perderás todos os recursos que investiste!',
                  target,
                  'Sim', 'Abortar'], 1);
      }
  
      function recruitmentSpeedUpCall() {
          var selectedValue = $('.js_reduceItemSelect').val();
          var inventory = [];
          if (parseInt(selectedValue) === 0 || !inventory[selectedValue]) {
              return;
          }
          var url = inventory[selectedValue]['activationUrl'];
          ajaxHandlerCall(url);
      }
  </script>

              };
              children[1].onclick = function (e) {

              var children = $(this).children();
